The room was comfortable with good places to store my stuff and still be able to move around. The bathroom was dated but just fine and right next to this room. I slept well on a good bed in this quiet location, and had a nice visit with another guest over breakfast in the morning. The breakfast wasn't anything special, but I was happy to have it. The location is perfect for using Eugene airport, and now that I know where I'm going, very easy to get to from the airport. I will definitely stay here again.</p><span data-reactid="600">Carol</span><span data-reactid="601">2016-12-06T00:00:00Z</span></li>

                         Beautiful and spacious private two-bedroom garden apartment in a stunning Southwest Hills home. Quiet neighborhood with lovely views of surrounding hills, minutes from the University of Oregon and Eugene’s main attractions. Features wifi, cable television, full kitchen and laundry, enticing garden, stunning views, private entry and parking. Comfortably furnished to meet the needs of up to six people.

                        <div data-reactid="1304">
                         Experience the majestic beauty of Eugene from your bright and airy home away from home. Nestled into a lush hillside amid a terraced flower garden, this private, two-bedroom suite will awe you with its panoramic views of the Southwest Hills’ incomparable natural landscape. Whether you’re visiting the University of Oregon, taking advantage of Tracktown USA’s many trails, attending an athletic event, or simply touring the Pacific Northwest, you will be in the ideal setting. Far from the hustle and bustle of the city but only four miles from the university and downtown, this is the perfect happy medium. The traditionally furnished apartment has two bedrooms, each with a queen-size bed, nightstands, a dresser, and a large closet. The combination living room, dining room, and kitchen includes comfortable seating, a dining table, a small desk, and a television with DVD player. The kitchen cabinets are stocked with all of the dishes, cookware, and utensils you need. Just outside the sliding glass doors you will find a covered patio furnished with two seating areas from which you can enjoy the garden and the magnificent mountain views. Features include a separate entrance, your own parking space, a small laundry room within the apartment, and all of the conveniences of home, such as wireless internet, iron and ironing board, toiletries, and extra linens. Please make your reservation today. A generous welcome basket awaits your arrival!

                        <div data-reactid="1438">
                         This room's décor was chosen by my granddaughters. It is their room when they visit me. It is bright and cheerful with plenty of room to move around.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1439">
                         My warm, ranch-style home in West Eugene has two private rooms--this listing has a bunk bed set. The bunk set consists of a twin on top, a full bed on the bottom, and a twin trundle bed underneath. A second bedroom has a single captain's bed (a separate listing available during summer months only). There is one shared bathroom in the house which has a tub/shower. Accommodations are best suited for 1 or 5 guests with the possibility (ask first) of additional guest(s) in the living room which contains a hide-a-bed that will sleep two comfortably. I have several pets. There is Mango, a cockatiel, who occupies space in the laundry room. She loves to be whistled and spoken to. She will mimic your whistles. In addition to Mango, is Oreo a black and white kitty who lives outdoors. She does come in the house to eat so the raccoons and neighbor cats do not get her food. She is very affection and loves attention. Oreo shares the backyard with Ruby and Kylo, two pet rabbits who enjoy eating carrots and greens from the garden.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1440">
                         My home is in a well-established moderate income neighborhood. It is quiet and very safe. While my neighbors keep to themselves most of the time, they are friendly. I am close to an extensive bike path system as well as a city park and recreation center. Peterson Barn Park and Echo Hollow Park and Swim Center are only a few minutes from my home.
                        </div>
